From the Golden Bridge, visitors can admire the pristine forests and the whole beautiful Da Nang city.\n\nOTHER ATTRACTIONS ON BA NA HILLS\nBesides the stunning Golden Bridge Ba Na Hills, there are many other alluring destinations you need to check out here.\n1.Le Jardin D\u2019amour Flower Gardens\u00a0\nThe maze of flower is not on the screen anymore when you first step into this marvelous garden. \u00a0Especially, Le Jardin D\u2019amour Flower gardens are divided into nine gardens with separate unique architectural design including: Suoi Mo garden, Eden Garden, Mysterious Garden, Couple Garden, Reflection Garden, The Mythical Garden, Memories Garden, Sacred Garden and Vineyard.\n2. 100 year old Wine Collar \u2013 Debay Wine Cellar\nNearby Le Jardin D\u2019amour Flower Gardens is the Debay Wine Cellar constructed by French in 1923. People here stored wine in oak barrels for years which brings about a feeling of nostalgic finest wine taste. Guests can come by and taste various types of fermented fruits and wine here, but prepare yourself not to get drunk before exploring other lovely attractions.\n3. The French Village\nInspired by the Renaissance Europe architecture, the French Village is considered to be a miniature Europe in the heart of Danang. With the unique architecture and cool air, this place will help local people here travel straight to the dreamy nostalgic European village with a complete complex of everything including a church, a square of fountain, shops, eateries and hotels.\n4. Linh Ung Pagoda\nBeing famous for the Giant White Buddha statue, Linh Ung pagoda located on top of Ba Na Hills with the height of nearby 1500m from sea level. Surrounded by a panoramic view overlooking Danang city, visitors can enjoy the tranquil and peaceful ambience here while indulge in the overwhelming sightseeing.\n5. Wax Museum\nNow move to somewhere much more entertain \u2013 Bana Hills Wax Museum. To visit this unique museum, you need to buy a ticket cost 100.000 VND.
